## Idea

The sign of a permutation is defined as the parity of the length of the decomposition of the permutation into transpositions. We show that each such decomposition as the same parity, so the sign map is well defined. We then show that the sign map is a group homomorphism.

## Definitions

### The sign homomorphism into ℤ/2

<pre class="Agda"><a id="5869" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="5876" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5876" class="Module">_</a>
  <a id="5880" class="Symbol">{</a><a id="5881" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5881" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5883" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5885" href="Agda.Primitive.html#597" class="Postulate">Level</a><a id="5890" class="Symbol">}</a> <a id="5892" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5893" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5893" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="5895" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5897" href="elementary-number-theory.natural-numbers.html#1458" class="Datatype">ℕ</a><a id="5898" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5900" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5901" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5901" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="5903" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5905" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5153" class="Function">UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="5918" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5881" class="Bound">l</a> <a id="5920" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5893" class="Bound">n</a><a id="5921" class="Symbol">)</a> 
  <a id="5926" class="Keyword">where</a>

  <a id="5935" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5935" class="Function">sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="5961" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="5963" href="foundation.automorphisms.html#1210" class="Function">Aut</a> <a id="5967" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="5968" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5248" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="5986" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5901" class="Bound">X</a><a id="5987" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="5989" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="5991" href="univalent-combinatorics.standard-finite-types.html#2149" class="Function">Fin</a> <a id="5995" class="Number">2</a>
  <a id="5999" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5935" class="Function">sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6025" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6025" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6027" class="Symbol">=</a>
    <a id="6033" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#605" class="Field">pr1</a> <a id="6037" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6038" href="foundation-core.contractible-types.html#1098" class="Function">center</a> <a id="6045" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6046" href="finite-group-theory.permutations.html#20688" class="Function">is-contr-parity-transposition-permutation</a> <a id="6088" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5893" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="6090" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5901" class="Bound">X</a> <a id="6092" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6025" class="Bound">f</a><a id="6093" class="Symbol">))</a>

  <a id="6099" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6099" class="Function">preserves-add-sign-homomorphism-Fin-two</a> <a id="6139" class="Symbol">:</a>
    <a id="6145" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6146" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6146" class="Bound">f</a> <a id="6148" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6148" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="6150" class="Symbol">:</a> <a id="6152" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6153" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5248" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6171" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5901" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6172" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="6174" href="foundation-core.equivalences.html#1621" class="Function Operator">≃</a> <a id="6176" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="6177" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5248" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="6195" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5901" class="Bound">X</a><a id="6196" class="Symbol">))</a> <a id="6199" class="Symbol">→</a>

      <a id="6626" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6628" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="6630" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6630" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="6632" class="Symbol">→</a>
        <a id="6642" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="6644" href="foundation-core.identity-types.html#4003" class="Function">ap</a>

                <a id="9345" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9347" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#515" class="Record">Σ</a> <a id="9349" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9350" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5248" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="9368" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5901" class="Bound">X</a><a id="9369" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9371" class="Symbol">(λ</a> <a id="9374" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9374" class="Bound">x</a> <a id="9376" class="Symbol">→</a> <a id="9378" href="foundation.decidable-propositions.html#2276" class="Function">type-decidable-Prop</a> <a id="9398" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9399" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9293" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9401" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9374" class="Bound">x</a><a id="9402" class="Symbol">)))))</a>
    <a id="9412" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9096" class="Function">list-trans</a> <a id="9423" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9423" class="Bound">f&#39;</a> <a id="9426" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9426" class="Bound">h</a> <a id="9428" class="Symbol">=</a>
      <a id="9436" href="finite-group-theory.permutations.html#17024" class="Function">list-transpositions-permutation-count</a> <a id="9474" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9475" href="univalent-combinatorics.finite-types.html#5248" class="Function">type-UU-Fin-Level</a> <a id="9493" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5901" class="Bound">X</a><a id="9494" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9496" class="Symbol">(</a><a id="9497" href="foundation-core.dependent-pair-types.html#588" class="InductiveConstructor">pair</a> <a id="9502" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#5893" class="Bound">n</a> <a id="9504" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9426" class="Bound">h</a><a id="9505" class="Symbol">)</a> <a id="9507" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9423" class="Bound">f&#39;</a>

      <a id="9579" href="univalent-combinatorics.lists.html#2156" class="Datatype">list</a>

            <a id="9652" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="9654" class="Symbol">λ</a> <a id="9656" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9656" class="Bound">P</a> <a id="9658" class="Symbol">→</a>

                <a id="10672" class="Symbol">(</a> <a id="10674" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#9096" class="Function">list-trans</a> <a id="10685" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#6368" class="Bound">g</a> <a id="10687" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#10019" class="Bound">h</a><a id="10688" class="Symbol">))</a>

### The sign homomorphism into the symmetric group S₂

<pre class="Agda"><a id="10759" class="Keyword">module</a> <a id="10766" href="finite-group-theory.sign-homomorphism.html#10766" class="Module">_</a>

## Deloopings of the sign homomorphism
